<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>It is a policy objective that:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the owner of a unit must not dispose of a unit by way of declaration of

trust; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if a purported disposal contravenes the rule in paragraph&#160;(a), it is

of no effect.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Beneficial interest in unit must not be transferred independently of legal interest_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(7)</dt><dd>It is a policy objective that:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a beneficial interest in a unit must not be transferred independently of

the legal interest in the unit; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if a purported transfer contravenes the rule in paragraph&#160;(a), it is

of no effect.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Definition_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(8)</dt><dd>In this clause:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_eligible entity_ means an entity included in a class of entities

declared by the SDA scheme to be entities who are eligible to become

transferees of units.

 </dl></dl>

37P  Making of SDA payments

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>It is a policy objective that, in accordance with the SDA scheme, lump sum

payments or quarterly payments will be paid to registered owners of units in

payment rights under the scheme.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>It is a policy objective that, if an SDA payment is due to be paid to an entity, the payment may be recovered, as a debt due to the entity, by action in a court of competent jurisdiction.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>It is a policy objective that, if an individual is entitled to receive an SDA payment and the payment has not been made at the date of the death of the individual, the amount of that payment is payable to the legal personal representative of the individual. </dd> </dl></dl>

37Q  Conferral of administrative powers etc.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The SDA scheme may make provision with respect to a matter by conferring

on the DAA, or the Minister, a power to make a decision of an administrative

character.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>If the SDA scheme confers on the Minister a power to make a decision of an administrative character, the scheme may also make provision for and in relation to the Minister delegating that power to the DAA. </dd> </dl></dl>

37R  Review of decisions

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The SDA scheme must contain provisions for and in relation to the review

of decisions of the DAA, or the Minister, under the scheme that affect an

entity.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>Those provisions must provide for review by the Administrative Appeals Tribunal or the Administrative Review Tribunal (as the case may be).</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>Subclause&#160;(2) does not limit subclause&#160;(1). </dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

37S  Fees

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The SDA scheme may provide for fees.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The amount of a fee under the SDA scheme must not be such as to amount to taxation. </dd> </dl></dl>

37T  Statutory declarations

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The SDA scheme may provide for statements in claims to be verified by

statutory declaration.

 </dl></dl>

37U  Methods by which SDA payments may be made

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The SDA scheme may make provision for the methods by which SDA payments

may be made.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The SDA scheme may require that SDA payments be made using an electronic funds transfer system.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>Subclause&#160;(2) does not limit subclause&#160;(1). </dd> </dl></dl>

37V  Adjustment of eligibility for payment rights etc.&#151;death

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The SDA scheme may make provision for and in relation to the adjustment of:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>eligibility for the grant of payment rights under the scheme; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the calculation of the face value of payment rights under the scheme;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

in relation to the death of an individual who would have otherwise been eligible to be granted a payment right under the SDA scheme.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	For example, the SDA scheme may contain provisions setting

out the eligibility of the trustee of the deceased estate, or of one or more

beneficiaries in the estate, to be granted a payment right under the scheme and

setting out the calculation of the face value of that right.

 </dl></dl>

37W  Ancillary or incidental provisions

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The SDA scheme may contain such ancillary or incidental provisions as the

Minister considers appropriate.

 </dl></dl>

37X  Scheme-making power not limited

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Clauses&#160;37C to 37W do not, by implication, limit clause&#160;37B.

 </dl></dl>

37Y  Variation of scheme

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The SDA scheme may be varied, but not revoked, in accordance with

subsection 33(3) of the _Acts Interpretation Act 1901_.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>Subclause&#160;(1) does not limit the application of subsection 33(3) of the _Acts Interpretation Act 1901_ to other instruments under this Act. </dd> </dl></dl>

37Z  Scheme to be a disallowable instrument

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		An instrument under clause&#160;37B is a disallowable instrument for the

purposes of section&#160;46A of the _Acts Interpretation Act 1901_.

 </dl></dl>

37ZA  Application to things happening before commencement

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The use of the present tense in a provision of this Division does not imply

that the provision does not apply to things happening before the commencement

of this Division.

 </dl></dl>

37ZB  Use and disclosure of information obtained under the DSAP scheme

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A record keeper who has possession or control of a record that contains

personal information that was obtained for the purposes of the administration

of the DSAP scheme may use the information, or disclose the information to a

person, body or agency, for the purposes of the administration of the SDA

scheme.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>Unless the contrary intention appears, an expression used in this clause has the same meaning as in the _Privacy Act 1988_. </dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

Division&#160;2&#151;Information-gathering powers 
 38  DAA may obtain information and documents 

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This clause applies to a person if the DAA has reason to believe that the

entity:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>has information or a document that is relevant to the operation of the

DSAP scheme or the SDA scheme; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>is capable of giving evidence which the DAA has reason to believe is

relevant to the operation of the DSAP scheme or the SDA scheme.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The DAA may, by written notice given to the person, require the person:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>to give to the DAA, within the period and in the manner and form specified

in the notice, any such information; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>to produce to the DAA, within the period and in the manner specified in

the notice, any such documents; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>to make copies of any such documents and to produce to the DAA, within the

period and in the manner specified in the notice, those copies; or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>if the person is an individual&#151;to appear before the DAA at a time and

place specified in the notice to give any such evidence, either orally or in

writing, and produce any such documents; or</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>if the person is a body corporate&#151;to cause a competent officer of the

body to appear before the DAA at a time and place specified in the notice to

give any such evidence, either orally or in writing, and produce any such

documents.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>A period specified under paragraph&#160;(2)(a), (b) or (c) must not be

shorter than 14 days after the notice is given.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>A time specified under paragraph&#160;(2)(d) or (e) must be at least 14 days after the notice is given.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>A person is guilty of an offence if: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person has been given a notice under subclause&#160;(2); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the person engages in conduct; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the person's conduct contravenes a requirement in the notice.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Penalty:	30 penalty units.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Chapter&#160;2 of the _Criminal Code_ sets out the

general principles of criminal responsibility.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>A notice under subclause&#160;(2) must set out the effect of the following

provisions:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>subclause&#160;(5);</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>clause&#160;133;</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>section&#160;136.1 of the _Criminal Code_;</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>section&#160;137.1 of the _Criminal Code_;</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>section&#160;137.2 of the _Criminal Code_.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

39  Copying documents&#151;reasonable compensation

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		A person is entitled to be paid reasonable compensation for complying with a

requirement covered by paragraph 38(2)(c).

 </dl></dl>

40  Self-incrimination

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>An individual is not excused from giving information or evidence or

producing a document or a copy of a document under this Division on the ground

that the information or evidence or the production of the document or copy

might tend to incriminate the individual or expose the individual to a

penalty.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>However: </dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>giving the information or evidence or producing the document or copy; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>any information, document or thing obtained as a direct or indirect

consequence of giving the information or evidence or producing the document or

copy;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

is not admissible in evidence against the individual in criminal proceedings other than:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>proceedings for an offence against subclause 38(5) or clause&#160;133;

or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>proceedings for an offence against section&#160;136.1, 137.1 or 137.2 of

the _Criminal Code_ that relates to this Division.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

41  Copies of documents

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The DAA may inspect a document or copy produced under this Division and

may make and retain copies of, or take and retain extracts from, such a

document.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The DAA may retain possession of a copy of a document produced in accordance with a requirement covered by paragraph 38(2)(c). </dd> </dl></dl>

42  DAA may retain documents

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The DAA may take, and retain for as long as is necessary, possession of a

document produced under this Division.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The person otherwise entitled to possession of the document is entitled to be supplied, as soon as practicable, with a copy certified by the DAA to be a true copy.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>The certified copy must be received in all courts and tribunals as evidence as if it were the original.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>Until a certified copy is supplied, the DAA must provide the person otherwise entitled to possession of the document, or a person authorised by that person, reasonable access to the document for the purposes of inspecting and making copies of, or taking extracts from, the document. </dd> </dl></dl>

Division&#160;3&#151;Protection of confidentiality of information 
 43  Protection of confidentiality of information

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This clause restricts what a person (the _entrusted person_)

may do with protected information, or protected documents, that the person has

obtained in the course of official employment.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The entrusted person: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>must not make a record of protected information; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>must not disclose it to anyone else;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

if the recording or disclosure is not in accordance with subclause&#160;(3).

Penalty:	Imprisonment for 2 years.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Chapter&#160;2 of the _Criminal Code_ sets out the

general principles of criminal responsibility.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>It is not an offence against subclause&#160;(2) if any of the following

apply to the recording or disclosure:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the recording or disclosure is for the purposes of this Part, the DSAP

scheme or the SDA scheme or is otherwise required by any law of the

Commonwealth;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the recording or disclosure happens in the course of the performance of

the duties of the entrusted person's official employment;</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the disclosure is not likely to enable the identification of a particular

entity;</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>both:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

	(i)	the disclosure is to an entity who had an eligible interest in a dairy farm enterprise at 6.30 pm on 28&#160;September 1999; and
 	(ii)	the information relates to that enterprise;

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>the recording or disclosure is in connection with the administration of:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

	(i)	the DEP scheme; or
 	(ii)	a provision of the _Farm Household Support Act 1992_ in so far as that provision relates to the DEP scheme;

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>the recording or disclosure is in connection with the administration of

dairy-type grants.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	A defendant bears an evidential burden in relation to a

matter in paragraph&#160;(3)(a), (b), (e) or (f)&#151;see subsection 13.3(3) of the

_Criminal Code_.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>Despite subsection 13.3(3) of the _Criminal Code_, the defendant

does not bear an evidential burden in relation to a matter in

paragraph&#160;(3)(c) or (d) of this clause.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>Unless it is necessary for the purposes of this Part, the DSAP scheme or the SDA scheme, the entrusted person is not to be required: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>to produce any protected document to a court; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>to disclose protected information to a court.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>In this clause:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_disclose_ means divulge or communicate. _official employment_ means:  </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>service as a DAA member; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the performance of services for the DAA; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the exercise of powers or performance of functions under a delegation by

the DAA.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_protected document_ means any document made or given under, or for

the purposes of, this Part, the DSAP scheme or the SDA scheme. _protected information_ means information that meets all the following conditions:  </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>it relates to the affairs of a person other than the entrusted person;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>it was obtained by the entrusted person, or by any other person, in the

course of official employment;</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>it was disclosed or obtained for the purposes of this Part, the DSAP

scheme or the SDA scheme.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_this Part_ includes any other provision of this Schedule in so far

as that other provision relates to this Part.

 </dl></dl>

Division&#160;4&#151;Recovery of scheme debts 
 44  Scheme debt

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		For the purposes of this Division, a _scheme debt_ is so much of

an amount paid, or purportedly paid, to an entity by way of a DSAP payment or

an SDA payment as represents an overpayment.

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

45  Scheme debts are debts due to the industry services body

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		A scheme debt is a debt due to the industry services body.

 </dl></dl>

46  Recovery by legal proceedings

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A scheme debt may be recovered by the DAA, on behalf of the industry

services body, by action in a court of competent jurisdiction.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>An action under subclause&#160;(1) may be instituted by the DAA in its official name. </dd> </dl></dl>

47  Recovery by set-off

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If an entity is liable to pay a scheme debt, the scheme debt may be deducted

from one or more DSAP payments or SDA payments that are payable to the entity,

and if the scheme debt is so deducted, the DSAP payment or SDA payment (as the

case may be) is taken to have been paid in full to the entity.

 </dl></dl>

48  Industry services body may collect money from a person who owes money to an entity

_What this clause does_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This clause allows for the collection of money from a person who owes

money to an entity that has a scheme debt.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_The DAA may give direction_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The DAA may direct a person (the _third party_) who owes, or

may later owe, money (the _available money_) to the entity to pay

some or all of the available money to the industry services body in accordance

with the direction. The DAA must give a copy of the direction to the entity.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Limit on directions_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The direction cannot require an amount to be paid to the industry services

body at a time before it becomes owing by the third party to the entity.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Third party to comply_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>The third party must comply with the direction.

</dd> </dl></dl>

Penalty:	20 penalty units.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Chapter&#160;2 of the _Criminal Code_ sets out the

general principles of criminal responsibility.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>The third party is not guilty of an offence against subclause&#160;(4) if

the third party complies with the direction so far as the third party is able

to do so.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	A defendant bears an evidential burden in relation to the

matter in subclause&#160;(5). See subsection 13.3(3) of the _Criminal Code_.

 </dl></dl>

_Court orders_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>If a person is convicted of an offence in relation to a refusal or failure

of the third party to comply with subclause&#160;(4), the court may (in

addition to imposing a penalty on the convicted person) order the convicted

person to pay to the industry services body an amount up to the amount involved

in the refusal or failure of the third party.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Indemnity_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(7)</dt><dd>Any payment made by the third party under this clause is taken to have

been made with the authority of the entity and of all other persons concerned,

and the third party is indemnified for the payment.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

_Notice_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(8)</dt><dd>If the whole of the scheme debt of the entity is discharged before any

payment is made by the third party, the DAA must immediately give notice to the

third party of that fact.</dd> <dt>(9)</dt><dd>If a part of the scheme debt of the entity is discharged before any payment is made by the third party, the DAA must: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>immediately give notice to the third party of that fact; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>make an appropriate variation to the direction; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>give a copy of the varied direction to the entity.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_When third party is taken to owe money_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(10)</dt><dd>The third party is taken to owe money to the entity if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>money is due or accruing by the third party to the entity; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the third party holds money for or on account of the entity; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the third party holds money on account of some other person for payment to

the entity; or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the third party has authority from some other person to pay money to the

entity;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

whether or not the payment of the money to the entity is dependent on a pre-condition that has not been fulfilled. 

49  Penalty for unpaid scheme debts

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If an amount of a scheme debt that is payable by an entity remains unpaid

after the day by which it must be paid, the entity is liable to a penalty at

the rate of 16% per year on the unpaid amount.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The penalty is calculated from the day on which the amount becomes due to be paid.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>The fact that a judgment is entered or given in a court for the payment of an amount of a scheme debt, or of a composite amount that includes an amount of a scheme debt, does not of itself cause the amount of a scheme debt to stop being unpaid for the purposes of this clause.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>If the judgment debt bears interest, the penalty payable under this clause is reduced (but not beyond nil) by the following amount: </dd> </dl></dl>

<sub> ![A graphic exists here.](http://www.comlaw.gov.au/Details/C2004C00120/Html/89CA70A54877DC91CA256F71004D2B0E/$FILE/1207.gif)</sub>

where:

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_scheme debt component_ means so much of the judgment debt as

consists of a scheme debt.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>For the purposes of this clause, the day on which a scheme debt is due to

be paid is the day on which the DSAP payment or SDA payment concerned was

paid.</dd> <dt>(6)</dt><dd>This clause does not apply to a scheme debt that is attributable (in whole or in part) to an error made by the DAA or the industry services body, where the DSAP payment or SDA payment concerned was received in good faith.</dd> <dt>(7)</dt><dd>The DSAP scheme or the SDA scheme (as the case may be) must empower the DAA to remit the whole or a part of an amount of penalty payable under this clause.</dd> <dt>(8)</dt><dd>A penalty payable under this clause may be recovered by the Commonwealth as a debt to the Commonwealth.</dd> <dt>(9)</dt><dd>This clause has no effect to the extent (if any) to which it imposes taxation (within the meaning of section&#160;55 of the Constitution). </dd> </dl></dl>

Division&#160;5&#151;Cancellation of units 
 50  Cancellation of units because of the making of a false statement

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>before a payment right was granted, an entity made a false statement to a

person who was exercising powers, or performing functions, under or in

connection with this Part, the DSAP scheme or the SDA scheme; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>either:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

	(i)	the payment right was granted because of the making of the false statement; or
 	(ii)	as a result of the making of the false statement, the face value of the payment right exceeds the proper amount of the face value;

the DSAP scheme or the SDA scheme (as the case may be) must authorise the DAA to:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>if subparagraph&#160;(b)(i) applies&#151;cancel all of the units in the

payment right; or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>if subparagraph&#160;(b)(ii) applies&#151;cancel the number of units in the

payment right worked out by:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

	(i)	dividing the number of whole dollars in the amount of the excess by 32; and
 	(ii)	if the result of the division is not a whole number&#151;rounding down the result to the nearest whole number (treating zero as a whole number).

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If a unit is cancelled as authorised under this clause, this Schedule and

the DSAP scheme or the SDA scheme (as the case may be) have, and are taken

always to have had, effect as if the unit was never in existence.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	This may result in an overpayment. For recovery of

overpayments, see Division&#160;4.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>In this clause:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_false statement_ means a statement (whether made orally, in a

document or in any other way) that:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>is false or misleading in a material particular; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>omits any matter or thing without which the statement is misleading in a

material particular.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

51  Cancellation of units because of an error made by the DAA

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the DAA made an error in relation to the grant of a payment right; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>clause&#160;50 does not apply; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>either:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

	(i)	the payment right would not have been granted if the DAA had not made that error; or
 	(ii)	the face value of the payment right exceeds the amount that would have been the amount of the face value if the DAA had not made that error;

the DSAP scheme or the SDA scheme (as the case may be) must authorise the DAA to:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>if subparagraph&#160;(c)(i) applies&#151;cancel all of the units in the

payment right; or</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>if subparagraph&#160;(c)(ii) applies&#151;cancel the number of units in the

payment right worked out by:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

	(i)	dividing the number of whole dollars in the amount of the excess by 32; and
 	(ii)	if the result of the division is not a whole number&#151;rounding down the result to the nearest whole number (treating zero as a whole number).

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The DSAP scheme or the SDA scheme (as the case may be) may provide that

the DAA is not to cancel a unit as authorised under this clause if the DAA is

satisfied that the entity, or each of the entities, who received a DSAP payment

or an SDA payment in respect of the unit acted in good faith.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>If a unit is cancelled as authorised under this clause, this Schedule and the DSAP scheme or the SDA scheme (as the case may be) have, and are taken always to have had, effect as if the unit was never in existence. </dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	This may result in an overpayment. For recovery of

overpayments, see Division&#160;4.

 </dl></dl>

52  Cancellation of unit because of a breach of an undertaking to assign the unit

_DSAP scheme_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an entity (the _first entity_) has given the DAA an

undertaking to assign a unit in a payment right under the DSAP scheme to an

eligible entity as mentioned in paragraph 21(4)(b); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the first entity breaches the undertaking; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the DAA gives the first entity a written notice directing the first entity

to comply with the undertaking before the end of the period of 60 days

beginning when the direction is given; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the first entity contravenes the direction;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the DSAP scheme must authorise the DAA to cancel the unit.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1A)</dt><dd>For the purposes of subclause&#160;(1), _eligible entity_ has

the same meaning as in clause&#160;21.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_SDA scheme_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1B)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an entity (the _first entity_) has given the DAA an

undertaking to assign a unit in a payment right under the SDA scheme to an

eligible entity as mentioned in paragraph 37N(3)(b); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the first entity breaches the undertaking; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the DAA gives the first entity a written notice directing the first entity

to comply with the undertaking before the end of the period of 60 days

beginning when the direction is given; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the first entity contravenes the direction;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the SDA scheme must authorise the DAA to cancel the unit.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1C)</dt><dd>For the purposes of subclause&#160;(1B), _eligible entity_ has the same meaning as in clause&#160;37N.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_When cancellation takes effect_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The cancellation of a unit as authorised under this clause takes effect at

the end of that 60-day period.

</dd> </dl></dl>

53  Cancellation of units when a dairy exit payment becomes payable

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an entity has been granted a payment right in relation to a dairy farm

enterprise; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>either:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

	(i)	a decision is made under the DEP scheme that the entity is qualified for a dairy exit payment in relation to the enterprise; or
 	(ii)	a decision is made under the farm help re-establishment grant scheme (within the meaning of the _Farm Household Support Act 1992_) that the entity is qualified for a dairy-type grant; and

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>immediately before the decision is made, the entity is the registered

owner of one or more unencumbered units in the payment right;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the DSAP scheme or the SDA scheme (as the case may be) must authorise the 
<center>Back to Top</center>
 DAA to cancel those units.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The cancellation of a unit as authorised under this clause takes effect

from the time when the decision mentioned in the relevant subparagraph of

paragraph&#160;(1)(b) is made.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>A reference in this clause to an _unencumbered unit_ is a reference to a unit in respect of which no charge is registered. </dd> </dl></dl>

54  Limit on cancellation or variation

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		A payment right or a unit must not be cancelled or varied otherwise than as

authorised under this Part.

 </dl></dl>

Division&#160;6&#151;Dairy Adjustment Authority 
 55  Dairy Adjustment Authority

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The Dairy Adjustment Authority is established.

 </dl></dl>

56  Functions

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The DAA has the following functions:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>such functions as are conferred on the DAA by or under:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

	(i)	the DSAP scheme or the SDA scheme; or
 	(ii)	this Schedule; or
 	(iii)	any other law of the Commonwealth;

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>to do anything incidental to or conducive to the performance of any of the

above functions.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

57  Powers

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The DAA has power to do all things necessary or convenient to be done for

or in connection with the performance of its functions.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The powers of the DAA under this clause include (but are not limited to) the power to enter into contracts and agreements on behalf of the Commonwealth. </dd> </dl></dl>

58  Phasing-down of the DAA

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The Minister may, by notice published in the _Gazette_, declare that

a specified time is the _first DAA phase-down time_ for the

purposes of this Division.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The effect of the notice is to reduce the number of DAA

members from 5 to 2&#151;see clause&#160;59.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The Minister may, by notice published in the _Gazette_, declare that

a specified time is the _second DAA phase-down time_ for the

purposes of this Division. The specified time must be after the first DAA

phase-down time.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The effect of the notice is to reduce the number of DAA

members from 2 to 1&#151;see clause&#160;59.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>A declaration under subclause&#160;(1) or (2) has effect accordingly. 

</dd> </dl></dl>

59  Membership of the DAA

_Before the first DAA phase-down time_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Before the first DAA phase-down time, the DAA consists of the following

members:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a Chair;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>2 industry members;</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>a government member;</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>one other member.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Between the first DAA phase-down time and the second DAA phase-down time_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>During the period:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>beginning at the first DAA phase-down time; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>ending at the second DAA phase-down time;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the DAA consists of the following members:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>a Chair;</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>one other member.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>A person who held office as a DAA member immediately before the first DAA

phase-down time is taken to vacate that office at that time. However, this

subclause does not prevent the person from being re-appointed with effect from

the first DAA phase-down time.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_After the second DAA phase-down time_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>After the second DAA phase-down time, the DAA consists of a single

member.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>If, after the second DAA phase-down time, there is no ordinary member of the DAA who holds office under subclause&#160;(4), the Secretary holds that office.</dd> <dt>(6)</dt><dd>A person who held office as a DAA member immediately before the second DAA phase-down time is taken to vacate that office at that time. However, this subclause does not prevent the person from being re-appointed with effect from the second DAA phase-down time. </dd> </dl></dl>

60  Qualifications of DAA members

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A person is not to be appointed as:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the DAA Chair; or </dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the DAA member referred to in paragraph 59(1)(d);

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

unless it appears to the Minister that the person has knowledge of, or experience in, one or more of the following fields:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>business management;</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>finance;</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>legal practice;</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>actuarial practice.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>A person is not to be appointed as an industry member unless it appears to

the Minister that the person has knowledge of, or experience in, the production

of dairy produce.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>A person is not to be appointed as the government member unless it appears to the Minister that the person has knowledge of, or experience in, either or both of the following fields: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the formulation of government policy;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>public administration.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

61  Appointment of DAA members

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The ordinary DAA members are to be appointed by the Minister by written

instrument.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>An ordinary DAA member is to be appointed for the period specified in the instrument of appointment.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>An ordinary DAA member holds office on a part-time basis.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>The performance of the functions of the DAA is not affected only because of there being a vacancy or vacancies in the membership of the DAA.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>The performance of the functions of the DAA is not affected only because of the reconstitution of the DAA at the first DAA phase-down time or the second DAA phase-down time. </dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

62  Procedures

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The regulations may prescribe:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the manner in which the DAA is to perform its functions; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the procedure to be followed at or in relation to meetings of the DAA,

including matters with respect to the following:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

	(i)	the convening of meetings of the DAA;
 	(ii)	the number of DAA members who are to constitute a quorum;
 	(iii)	the selection of a DAA member to preside at meetings of the DAA in the absence of the DAA Chair; and
 	(iv)	the manner in which questions arising at a meeting of the DAA are to be decided.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>A resolution is taken to have been passed at a meeting of the DAA if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>without meeting, a majority of DAA members indicate agreement with the

resolution in accordance with the method determined by the DAA under

subclause&#160;(3); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>all DAA members were informed of the proposed resolution, or reasonable

efforts had been made to inform all DAA members of the proposed resolution.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>Subclause&#160;(2) applies only if the DAA:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>determines that it applies; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>determines the method by which DAA members are to indicate agreement with

resolutions.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>This clause does not apply after the second DAA phase-down time.

</dd> </dl></dl>

63  Disclosure of interests before the second DAA phase-down time

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>An ordinary DAA member who has a material personal interest in a matter

being considered by the DAA must, as soon as possible after the relevant facts

have come to the member's knowledge, disclose the nature of the interest at a

meeting of the DAA.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The disclosure is to be recorded in the minutes of the meeting and unless the Minister or the DAA otherwise determines, the DAA member must not: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>be present during any deliberation by the DAA about that matter; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>take part in any decision of the DAA relating to that matter.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>For the purposes of the making of a determination by the DAA under

subclause&#160;(2) in relation to a DAA member who has made a disclosure under

subclause&#160;(1), a DAA member who has an interest in the matter to which the

disclosure relates must not:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>be present during any deliberation of the DAA for the purposes of making

the determination; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>take part in the making by the DAA of the determination.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>This clause does not apply after the second DAA phase-down time.

</dd> </dl></dl>

64  Disclosure of interests after the second DAA phase-down time

_DAA to notify business interests to Minister_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The DAA must give written notice to the Minister of all material personal

interests that the DAA has or acquires in any business, or in any body

corporate carrying on a business.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

_DAA to notify potential conflict of interest to Minister_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If the DAA has a material personal interest in a matter being considered

or about to be considered by the DAA, the DAA must:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>give written notice to the Minister of that interest; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>take no further action on the matter before:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

	(i)	the end of 28 days after the date on which the Minister receives the notice; or
 	(ii)	the date on which written advice of a decision of the Minister under subclause&#160;(4) is given in relation to the matter;

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

 		whichever first occurs.

</dl></dl></dl>

_Minister may direct DAA to delegate_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the DAA has a material personal interest in a matter being considered or

about to be considered by the DAA; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the Minister considers that the interest could conflict with the proper

performance of the DAA's functions in relation to that matter;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

then:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the Minister must give the DAA a written notice directing the DAA:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

	(i)	not to deal with the matter personally; and
 	(ii)	to delegate the DAA's functions and powers in relation to that matter to a specified person under clause&#160;73; and
 	(iii)	not to delegate the DAA's functions and powers in relation to that matter to any other person; and

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the DAA must comply with the direction.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Minister may allow DAA to deal with matter personally_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the DAA has a material personal interest in a matter being considered or

about to be considered by the DAA; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the Minister does not consider that the interest could conflict with the

proper performance of the DAA's functions in relation to that matter;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the Minister may give the DAA a written notice stating that the Minister has no objection to the DAA dealing with the matter personally.

_Minister&apos;s direction to be given within 28 days of notification of DAA&apos;s interest_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the DAA has a material personal interest in a matter being considered or

about to be considered by the DAA; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the Minister considers that the interest could conflict with the proper

performance of the DAA's functions in relation to that matter; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the DAA gives written notice to the Minister of that interest under

subclause&#160;(2);

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

a direction under subclause&#160;(3) in relation to that matter has no effect unless it is given before the end of 28 days after the date on which the Minister receives the notice.

_Application_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>This clause does not apply before the second DAA phase-down time.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

65  Remuneration and allowances

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>An ordinary DAA member is to be paid such remuneration as is determined by

the Remuneration Tribunal.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>If no determination of that remuneration is in operation, a DAA member is to be paid such remuneration as is prescribed.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>An ordinary DAA member is to be paid such allowances as are prescribed.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>This clause has effect subject to the _Remuneration Tribunal Act 1973_. </dd> </dl></dl>

66  Leave of absence

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The Minister or the DAA Chair may grant leave to an ordinary DAA member to

be absent from a meeting or meetings of the DAA.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>This clause does not apply after the second DAA phase-down time. </dd> </dl></dl>

67  Resignation

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		An ordinary DAA member may resign by writing signed by the member and sent to

the Minister.

 </dl></dl>

68  Termination of appointment

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The Minister may terminate an ordinary DAA member's appointment if the

Minister is of the opinion that the member's performance has been

unsatisfactory.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The Minister may terminate the appointments of all of the ordinary DAA members if the Minister is of the opinion that the DAA's performance has been unsatisfactory.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>The Minister may terminate the appointment of an ordinary DAA member because of misbehaviour or physical or mental incapacity.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>If: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an ordinary DAA member becomes bankrupt, applies to take the benefit of

any law for the relief of bankrupt or insolvent debtors, compounds with

creditors or makes an assignment of remuneration for their benefit; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>an ordinary DAA member is absent, except on leave of absence, from 3

consecutive meetings of the DAA; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>an ordinary DAA member fails, without reasonable excuse, to comply with

clause&#160;63 or 64;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the Minister may terminate the appointment of the member.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>The Minister may at any time terminate the appointment of the government

member of the DAA.</dd> <dt>(6)</dt><dd>The Minister may at any time terminate the appointment of an ordinary DAA member who holds office under subclause 59(4). </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Subclause 59(4) deals with the ordinary DAA member who

holds office after the second DAA phase-down time.

 </dl></dl>

69  Other terms and conditions

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		An ordinary DAA member holds office on such terms and conditions (if any) in

respect of matters not provided for by this Act as are determined by the

Minister.

 </dl></dl>

70  Industry services body must provide assistance to DAA

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The industry services body must, if requested to do so by the DAA, make

available to the DAA reasonable resources and facilities (including secretariat

services, clerical assistance and computer resources) for the purposes of

enabling the DAA to perform its functions.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>If the services of an employee of the industry services body are made available to the DAA under subclause&#160;(1), the employee is not subject to the direction of the industry services body in relation to the provision of those services.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>Subclause&#160;(1) does not, by implication, prevent the DAA from obtaining resources and facilities otherwise than from the industry services body. </dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

71  Consultants etc.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The DAA may, on behalf of the Commonwealth, engage persons to give advice

to, and perform services for, the DAA.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The terms and conditions of engagement are as determined by the DAA. </dd> </dl></dl>

72  Delegation by DAA&#151;before second DAA phase-down time

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The DAA may, by resolution, delegate to:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a DAA member; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a senior employee of the industry services body;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

all or any of the DAA's functions and powers.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>A delegation of a function or power under this clause:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>may be revoked by resolution of the DAA (whether or not constituted by the

persons constituting the DAA at the time when the function or power was

delegated); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>continues in force notwithstanding a change in the membership of the DAA.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>Section&#160;34A of the _Acts Interpretation Act 1901_ applies in

relation to a delegation under this clause as if the DAA were a person.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>A certificate signed by the DAA Chair stating any matter with respect to a delegation of a function or power under this clause is prima facie evidence of that matter.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>A document purporting to be a certificate mentioned in subclause&#160;(4) is, unless the contrary is established, taken to be such a certificate and to have been duly given.</dd> <dt>(6)</dt><dd>A delegate under this clause is, in the exercise of a function or power delegated under this clause, subject to any directions given by the DAA.</dd> <dt>(7)</dt><dd>A reference in this clause to a _senior employee of the industry services body_ is a reference to a person who: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>is an employee of the industry services body; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>holds or performs the duties of a position of General Manager.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(8)</dt><dd>This clause does not apply after the second DAA phase-down time.

</dd> </dl></dl>

73  Delegation by DAA&#151;after second DAA phase-down time

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The DAA may, by writing, delegate to an SES employee or acting SES

employee all or any of the DAA's functions and powers.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>A delegate under this clause is, in the exercise of a function or power delegated under this clause, subject to any directions given by the DAA.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>This clause does not apply before the second DAA phase-down time. </dd> </dl></dl>

74  Annual report

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The DAA must, as soon as practicable after the end of each financial year:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>prepare a report on its operations during that financial year; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>give the report to the Minister.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The Minister must cause a copy of the report to be laid before each House

of the Parliament within 15 sittings days of that House after the day on which

the Minister receives the report.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>This clause does not apply in relation to a financial year if: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the financial year is earlier than the 2000-2001 financial year; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the Secretary was the sole member of the DAA throughout the financial year.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

Division&#160;7&#151;Miscellaneous 
 75  DSAP and SDA payments taken to be subsidies for the purposes of section&#160;15-10 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		To avoid doubt, for the purposes of section&#160;15-10 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_, a DSAP payment or an SDA payment received by an entity

is taken to be a subsidy received by the entity in relation to carrying on a

business.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section&#160;15-10 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ provides that an entity's assessable income includes a subsidy

received in relation to carrying on a business.

 </dl></dl>

76  Review in 2002-2003

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>During the 2002-2003 financial year, the DAA must conduct a review of, and

make recommendations to the Minister about, the adequacy of collections of

dairy adjustment levy to fund DSAP payments, SDA payments and dairy exit

payments.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The DAA must prepare a report of a review and recommendations under subclause&#160;(1), and give the report to the Minister.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>The Minister must cause copies of a report to be laid before each House of the Parliament within 15 sittings days of that House after the completion of the preparation of the report.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>In this clause: </dd> </dl></dl>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_dairy adjustment levy_ means levy within the meaning of

Part&#160;4.

 </dl></dl>

Part&#160;3&#151;Dairy Structural Adjustment Fund

77  Establishment of the Dairy Structural Adjustment Fund

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A fund to be known as the Dairy Structural Adjustment Fund is established.

</dd> </dl></dl>

77A  The industry services body to keep the Dairy Structural Adjustment Fund

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The industry services body must keep and administer the Dairy Structural

Adjustment Fund.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The assets of the Dairy Structural Adjustment Fund are the property of the industry services body, but must be kept separate from all other property and must be held on trust by the body for the purposes of this Part.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>No stamp duty or other tax is payable under a law of a State or Territory in respect of the operation of subclause&#160;(2). </dd> </dl></dl>

77B  What the Dairy Structural Adjustment Fund consists of

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The Dairy Structural Adjustment Fund consists of the following:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>money credited to the Fund under clause&#160;78;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>investments the industry services body has as a result of investing money

in the Fund under clause&#160;79B;</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>all other money and property lawfully paid into, or forming part of, the

Fund.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

77C  Power to borrow or raise money for the purposes of the Dairy Structural Adjustment Fund

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The industry services body may:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>borrow money; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>raise money otherwise than by borrowing;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

for the purpose of making payments for which money of the Dairy Structural Adjustment Fund may be expended.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The meaning of _raise money otherwise than by borrowing_ is affected by clause&#160;77CC.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The industry services body may give security, including over the assets of

the Dairy Structural Adjustment Fund, in respect of the body's obligations in

relation to a borrowing or other raising of money under subclause&#160;(1).

</dd> </dl></dl>

77CA  Borrowing or raising money by dealing in securities

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Without limiting subclause 77C(1), the industry services body may, under

that subclause, borrow money, or raise money otherwise than by borrowing, by

dealing with securities.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>In this clause: </dd> </dl></dl>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_dealing with securities_ includes:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>creating, executing, entering into, drawing, making, accepting, endorsing,

issuing, discounting, selling, purchasing or re-selling securities; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>creating, selling, purchasing or re-selling rights or options in respect

of securities; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>entering into agreements or other arrangements relating to securities.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_securities_ includes stocks, debentures, debenture stocks, notes,

bonds, promissory notes, bills of exchange and similar instruments or documents.

 </dl></dl>

77CB  Hedging through currency contracts etc.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This clause applies to the following contracts:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>currency contracts;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>interest rate contracts;</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>futures contracts;</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>contracts relating to:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

	(i)	dealings known as currency swaps; or
 	(ii)	dealings known as interest rate swaps;

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>contracts relating to both of the dealings referred to in

paragraph&#160;(d);</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>options (including futures options).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The industry services body may enter into and deal with contracts to which

this clause applies for hedging purposes in relation to a borrowing or raising,

or a proposed borrowing or raising, of money under subclause 77C(1).</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>A contract is taken to be entered into or dealt with for hedging purposes only if the contract is entered into or dealt with for the purpose of managing the risk of variations in the costs of a borrowing or raising, or a proposed borrowing or raising, of money under subclause 77C(1).</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>In this clause: </dd> </dl></dl>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_currency contract means_:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a forward exchange rate contract; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a contract with respect to currency futures.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_futures contract means_:

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a deferred delivery contract; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a contract with respect to financial futures; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>a contract with respect to commodity futures.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

77CC  Obtaining credit etc. taken to be raising of an amount of money, otherwise than by borrowing

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This clause applies if the industry services body:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>does a thing mentioned in the table in subclause&#160;(2); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>does not do that thing in relation to a transaction that is in the

ordinary course of its day-to-day operations.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>By doing that thing, the industry services body is taken, for the purposes

of this Part and subclause 94(2), to raise the relevant amount of money

mentioned in the following table, otherwise than by borrowing:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<table><tr align="left">
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>Circumstances where the industry services body is taken to raise an amount of money, otherwise than by borrowing</div>

  </th>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>Item</div>

  </th>
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>If the industry services body...</div>

  </th>
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>by doing so, it is taken to raise this amount of money, otherwise than by borrowing...</div>

  </th>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>1</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>issues an instrument acknowledging a debt in consideration of the payment or deposit of money</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>the amount of the money paid or deposited</div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>2</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>issues an instrument acknowledging a debt in consideration of the provision of credit</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>the value of the credit provided</div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>3</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>obtains credit</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>the value of the credit obtained</div>

  </td>
</tr></table>77D  Funding contract may include provisions relating to the Dairy Structural Adjustment Fund

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		A funding contract with the industry services body may include provisions

relating to the Dairy Structural Adjustment Fund. This clause does not

impliedly limit the matters that may be included in the contract.

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

78  Money to be paid into the Dairy Structural Adjustment Fund

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The following money is to be credited to the Dairy Structural Adjustment Fund:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>money paid to the industry services body under clause&#160;83 (which deals

with dairy adjustment levy);</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>money paid to the industry services body under clause&#160;84 (which deals

with fees under the DSAP scheme or the SDA scheme);</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>money paid to the industry services body under clause&#160;85 (which deals

with civil penalties relating to the DSAP scheme or the SDA scheme);</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>money paid to the industry services body by way of the recovery of a

scheme debt (within the meaning of clause&#160;44);</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>money paid to the industry services body under clause&#160;48 (which deals

with the collection of money from a person who owes money to an entity that has

a scheme debt);</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>money paid to the industry services body under subsection 56(3) of the

_Farm Household Support Act 1992_ (which deals with the recovery of

overpaid dairy exit payments);</dd>

<dt>(fa)</dt><dd>money paid to the industry services body under subsection 56(2A) of the

_Farm Household Support Act 1992_(which deals with the recovery of

overpaid dairy-type grants);</dd>

<dt>(g)</dt><dd>money received by the industry services body as interest or profits from

the investment of money standing to the credit of the Dairy Structural

Adjustment Fund;</dd>

<dt>(h)</dt><dd>money borrowed or otherwise raised by the industry services body for the

purpose of making payments for which money of the Dairy Structural Adjustment

Fund may be expended;</dd>

<dt>(ha)</dt><dd>money received by the industry services body in respect of contracts

entered into or dealt with by it under clause&#160;77CB;</dd>

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>money paid to the industry services body for the purposes of the Dairy

Structural Adjustment Fund.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

79  Application of the Dairy Structural Adjustment Fund

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Money standing to the credit of the Dairy Structural Adjustment Fund is to be

expended:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>in making DSAP payments; and</dd>

<dt>(aa)</dt><dd>in making SDA payments; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>in making dairy exit payments; and</dd>

<dt>(ba)</dt><dd>in making dairy-type grants; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>in reimbursing or meeting the expenses of the Commonwealth or the industry

services body incurred (whether before or after the commencement of this

clause) in relation to the development and implementation of the measures that

from time to time form part of the Dairy Industry Adjustment Package; and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>in meeting the expenses of the Commonwealth incurred in relation to:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

	(i)	the collection and recovery of amounts referred to in clause&#160;83 (which deals with dairy adjustment levy); or
 	(ii)	the administration of clause&#160;83; and

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>in payment of any remuneration and allowances of ordinary DAA members;

and</dd>

<dt>(g)</dt><dd>in meeting the expenses of the industry services body incurred in making

available to the DAA resources and facilities as mentioned in subclause 70(1);

and</dd>

<dt>(h)</dt><dd>in meeting the expenses incurred by the Commonwealth in relation to the

engagement of persons under clause&#160;71 (which deals with consultants to the

DAA); and</dd>

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>in meeting any other expenses incurred by the Commonwealth in relation to:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

	(i)	the administration of this Schedule, the DSAP scheme or the SDA scheme; or
 	(ii)	the performance of the functions, or the exercise of the powers, of the DAA; and

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(j)</dt><dd>in meeting the expenses incurred by the Commonwealth in relation to:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

	(i)	the administration of the DEP scheme; or
 	(ii)	the administration of the provisions of the _Farm Household Support Act 1992_ in so far as those provisions relate to the DEP scheme; and

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(ja)</dt><dd>in meeting the expenses incurred by the Commonwealth in relation to the

administration of dairy-type grants; and</dd>

<dt>(l)</dt><dd>in meeting the expenses of the industry services body incurred in

administering the Dairy Structural Adjustment Fund; and</dd>

<dt>(m)</dt><dd>in repaying money borrowed or otherwise raised for the purpose of making

payments for which money of the Dairy Structural Adjustment Fund may be

expended; and</dd>

<dt>(n)</dt><dd>in meeting the expenses of the industry services body incurred in

borrowing or otherwise raising money for the purpose of making payments for

which money of the Dairy Structural Adjustment Fund may be expended; and</dd>

<dt>(na)</dt><dd>in meeting the obligations and liabilities of the industry services body

in respect of contracts entered into or dealt with by it under

clause&#160;77CB; and</dd>

<dt>(nb)</dt><dd>in meeting the expenses of the industry services body incurred in respect

of contracts entered into or dealt with by it under clause&#160;77CB; and</dd>

<dt>(nc)</dt><dd>in payment of amounts relating to the indemnity mentioned in

clause&#160;86A; and</dd>

<dt>(o)</dt><dd>in reimbursing the Commonwealth for amounts that are refunded under

clause&#160;124 (which deals with dairy adjustment levy); and</dd>

<dt>(p)</dt><dd>in reimbursing the Commonwealth for amounts that are refunded under

regulations made for the purposes of clause&#160;125 (which deals with dairy

adjustment levy); and</dd>

<dt>(q)</dt><dd>in making payments under the Dairy Regional Assistance Programme; and</dd>

<dt>(r)</dt><dd>in meeting the expenses of the Commonwealth incurred in relation to the

administration of the Dairy Regional Assistance Programme.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	For the Dairy Regional Assistance Programme, see

clause&#160;86.

 </dl></dl>

79A  How money is to be kept

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Money in the Dairy Structural Adjustment Fund must:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>until applied for the purposes of this Part; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>until invested under clause&#160;79B;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

be kept by the industry services body in an account or accounts with an Australian ADI separate from any account or accounts in which other money is kept.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>In this clause:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_Australian ADI_ means:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an ADI (authorised deposit-taking institution) within the meaning of the

_Banking Act 1959_; or</dd>

<dt>(aa)</dt><dd>the Reserve Bank of Australia; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a person who carries on State banking within the meaning of paragraph

51(xiii) of the Constitution.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

79B  Money in Dairy Structural Adjustment Fund may be invested

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Money in the Dairy Structural Adjustment Fund that is not immediately

required for the purposes of this Part may be invested in any way in which

trustees are for the time being authorised by a law in force in a State or

Territory to invest trust funds.

 </dl></dl>

79C  Report to Minister

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The industry services body must, as soon as practicable after 30&#160;June

in each year, prepare and give to the Minister a report on the administration

of the Dairy Structural Adjustment Fund during the year that ended on that

30&#160;June.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The Minister must cause a copy of each report to be tabled in each House of the Parliament within 15 sitting days of that House after the day on which the Minister receives the report. </dd> </dl></dl>

80  Solvency of the Dairy Structural Adjustment Fund

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The industry services body and the Minister must take all reasonable steps to

ensure that there is sufficient money in the Dairy Structural Adjustment Fund

to:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>make DSAP payments, SDA payments, dairy exit payments and dairy-type

grants as they fall due; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>meet any other calls on that Fund as those calls fall due.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

83  Payment of dairy adjustment levy to the industry services body

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The Commonwealth must pay to the industry services body an amount equal to

each amount received by the Commonwealth by way of:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>dairy adjustment levy; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>penalty payable under clause&#160;107.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The Commonwealth must pay to the industry services body an amount equal to

each amount of dairy adjustment levy notionally received by the Commonwealth

under clause&#160;131.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>The Consolidated Revenue Fund is appropriated for the purposes of subclauses&#160;(1) and (2).</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>In this clause: </dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_dairy adjustment levy_ means levy within the meaning of Part&#160;4.

 </dl></dl>

84  Payment of DSAP and SDA scheme fees to the industry services body

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The Commonwealth must pay to the industry services body an amount equal to

each amount received by the Commonwealth by way of a fee under the DSAP scheme

or the SDA scheme.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The Consolidated Revenue Fund is appropriated for the purposes of subclause&#160;(1). </dd> </dl></dl>

85  Payment of penalties under the DSAP scheme and SDA scheme to the industry services body

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The Commonwealth must pay to the industry services body an amount equal to

each amount received by the Commonwealth by way of a penalty under

clause&#160;49.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The Consolidated Revenue Fund is appropriated for the purposes of subclause&#160;(1). </dd> </dl></dl>

86  Dairy Regional Assistance Programme

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>For the purposes of this Part, the _Dairy Regional Assistance Programme_ is a part of the Regional Assistance Programme, being the

part known as the Dairy Regional Assistance Programme.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>To avoid doubt, the Department of Employment, Workplace Relations and Small Business is responsible for administering the Dairy Regional Assistance Programme. This includes (but is not limited to) responsibility for determining: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the recipients of payments; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the amounts of payments; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the timing of payments; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the terms and conditions of payments.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>The total amount paid out of the Dairy Structural Adjustment Fund:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>in making payments under the Dairy Regional Assistance Programme; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>in meeting the expenses of the Commonwealth incurred in relation to the

administration of the Dairy Regional Assistance Programme;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

must not exceed $65 million.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>In this clause:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_Regional Assistance Programme_ means the Programme administered by

the Commonwealth and known as the Regional Assistance Programme.

 </dl></dl>

86A  Industry services body entitled to full indemnity

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The industry services body is entitled to be fully indemnified against any

liability (including any liability as to costs) incurred by it in keeping and

administering, or purporting to keep and administer, the Dairy Structural

Adjustment Fund.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The indemnity is to be paid out of the assets of the Dairy Structural Adjustment Fund. </dd> </dl></dl>

Part&#160;4&#151;Collection of dairy adjustment levy 
 Division&#160;1&#151;Introduction 
 87  Simplified outline

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The following is a simplified outline of this Part:

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

*	The principal levy base for dairy adjustment levy is the sale of a leviable milk product to a person who purchases for the purposes of resale in Australia, where the resale is a retail sale.

*	Dairy adjustment levy is imposed by the separate Dairy Adjustment Levy Acts, and the rate of levy is set out in those Acts.

*	Levy may be collected by collection agents and collection sub-agents. 

88  Definitions

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		In this Part, unless the contrary intention appears:

 </dl></dl>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_authorised person_ means an APS employee who has been authorised

by the Secretary under clause&#160;127 for the purposes of the provision in

which the expression occurs. _collecting organisation_ means an organisation that is a party to an agreement under clause&#160;103\. _collection agent_ means a person who, under clause&#160;97, is an agent of the Commonwealth for the purposes of the collection of levy. _collection sub-agent_ means a person who, under clause&#160;98 or 99, is a sub-agent of the Commonwealth for the purposes of the collection of levy. _dairy product_ means:  </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>milk; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>any other product made from, or containing, milk or a constituent part of

milk.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_designated small levy-payer_ has the meaning given by

clause&#160;123\. _designated small remitter_ has the meaning given by clause&#160;122\. _examinable documents_ means any documents relevant to the operation of this Part. _late payment penalty_ means penalty payable under clause&#160;107\. _leviable milk product_ means a dairy product that is:  </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>marketed principally as:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

	(i)	a beverage for human consumption; or
 	(ii)	an ingredient for use in making a beverage for human consumption; or

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>for use principally as:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

	(i)	a beverage for human consumption; or
 	(ii)	an ingredient for use in making a beverage for human consumption;

but does not include a product declared by the regulations to be exempt from levy.

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_levy_ means levy that is payable under Division&#160;2 and imposed

as dairy adjustment levy by any of the following:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the _Dairy Adjustment Levy (Excise) Act 2000_;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the _Dairy Adjustment Levy (Customs) Act 2000_;</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the _Dairy Adjustment Levy (General) Act 2000_.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_organisation_ includes an unincorporated body of persons. _premises_ includes:  </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a structure, building, aircraft, vehicle or vessel; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a place (whether enclosed or built on or not); and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>a part of premises (including premises of the kind referred to in

paragraph&#160;(a) or (b)).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_process_, in relation to a leviable milk product, means:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the production of the product; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the importation into Australia of the product; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the performance of any other operation in relation to the product;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

but does not include:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the chilling of the product; or</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>the performance of any operation specified in the regulations.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_relevant application to own use_, in relation to a

leviable milk product, means _:_

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>giving the product away; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>transferring property in the product under a contract that is not a

contract of sale; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>using the product as an ingredient in making a beverage or other product,

where:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

	(i)	the beverage or other product is for supply directly to a consumer; or
 	(ii)	the beverage or other product is to be given away; or
 	(iii)	property in the beverage or other product is to be transferred under a contract that is not a contract of sale.

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_State_ includes the Australian Capital Territory and the Northern

Territory.

 </dl></dl>

Division&#160;2&#151;Liability for levy 
 89  When levy is payable

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Levy is payable on each of the following:

</dd> </dl></dl>
