<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the sale of a leviable milk product to a person who purchases for the

purposes of resale in Australia, where the resale is a retail sale; </dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the retail sale of a leviable milk product; </dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the sale of a leviable milk product to a person who purchases for the

purpose of relevantly applying the product to the person's own use in

Australia; </dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the relevant application to a person's own use of a leviable milk product.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>Paragraph&#160;(1)(d) does not apply to the relevant application to a

person's own use of a leviable milk product if the product is consumed at the

site on which it was produced.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>Levy is not payable under this Division unless it is imposed as dairy adjustment levy by another Act. </dd> </dl></dl>

90  Commencement of levy

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Levy is not payable under paragraph 89(1)(a), (b) or (c) on the sale of a

leviable milk product if the sale occurs before 8&#160;July 2000.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>Levy is not payable under paragraph 89(1)(d) on the relevant application to a person's own use of a leviable milk product if the relevant application occurs before 8&#160;July 2000\. </dd> </dl></dl>

91  No double levy

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Levy is not payable in respect of a leviable milk product if levy has

previously been imposed in respect of that product.

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

92  Exemptions from levy

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The regulations may make provision for exemptions from levy.

 </dl></dl>

93  Who pays the levy

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Levy payable under paragraph 89(1)(a) is payable by the person who

purchased the leviable milk product for the purposes of resale.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>Levy payable under paragraph 89(1)(b) is payable by the person who is the retail seller of the leviable milk product.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>Levy payable under paragraph 89(1)(c) is payable by the person who purchased the leviable milk product for the purpose of relevantly applying the product to the person's own use.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>Levy payable under paragraph 89(1)(d) is payable by the person who relevantly applied the leviable milk product to the person's own use. </dd> </dl></dl>

94  Termination of levy when core funding obligations are met

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The Minister may, by notice published in the _Gazette_, declare that

the 28th day after the day of the publication of the notice is the _levy termination day_ for the purposes of this clause.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The Minister must not make a declaration under subclause&#160;(1) unless the Minister is satisfied that there is no reasonable likelihood of money being paid out of the Dairy Structural Adjustment Fund, at any time after that 28th day, for any of the following purposes: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>making DSAP payments;</dd>

<dt>(aa)</dt><dd>making SDA payments;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>making dairy exit payments;</dd>

<dt>(ba)</dt><dd>making dairy-type grants;</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>repaying money borrowed or otherwise raised for the purpose of making

payments for which money in the Dairy Structural Adjustment Fund may be

expanded;</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>meeting the expenses of the industry services body incurred in borrowing

or otherwise raising money for the purposes of making payments for which money

in the Dairy Structural Adjustment Fund may be expanded;</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>in meeting the obligations and liabilities of the industry services body

in respect of contracts entered into or dealt with by it under

clause&#160;77CB;</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>in meeting the expenses of the industry services body incurred in respect

of contracts entered into or dealt with by it under clause&#160;77CB.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>Levy is not payable under paragraph 89(1)(a), (b) or (c) on the sale of a

leviable milk product if the sale occurs after the levy termination day.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>Levy is not payable under paragraph 89(1)(d) on the relevant application to a person's own use of a leviable milk product if the relevant application occurs after the levy termination day. </dd> </dl></dl>

95  Termination of levy if DSAP payment start day does not occur within 6 months after the _Dairy Industry Adjustment Act 2000_ receives Royal Assent

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This clause applies if the DSAP payment start day is not fixed by a

Proclamation published in the _Gazette_ within the period of 6 months

beginning on the day on which the _Dairy Industry Adjustment Act 2000_

receives the Royal Assent.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>Levy is not payable under paragraph 89(1)(a), (b) or (c) on the sale of a leviable milk product if the sale occurs after the end of that period.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>Levy is not payable under paragraph 89(1)(d) on the relevant application to a person's own use of a leviable milk product if the relevant application occurs after the end of that period. </dd> </dl></dl>

Division&#160;3&#151;When levy due for payment 
 96  When levy due for payment

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Levy payable under paragraph 89(1)(a) or (c) on the sale of a leviable

milk product is due and payable on whichever is the earlier of the following

days:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the first day on which any part of the consideration for the sale is

due;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the 90th day after the day on which the sale occurred.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>Levy payable by a person under paragraph 89(1)(b) on the retail sale of a

leviable milk product is due and payable on:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the person is a designated small levy-payer in relation to the

financial year in which the retail sale occurred&#151;the 28th day after the end of

the financial year; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>in any other case&#151;the 28th day after the end of the month in which the

retail sale occurred.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>Levy payable by a person under paragraph 89(1)(d) on the relevant

application to the person's own use of a leviable milk product is due and

payable on:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the person is a designated small levy-payer in relation to the

financial year in which the relevant application occurred&#151;the 28th day after

the end of the financial year; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>in any other case&#151;the 28th day after the end of the month in which the

relevant application occurred.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Division&#160;4&#151;Collection agents, collection sub-agents and collecting organisations 
 97  Collection agents 

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This clause applies to levy if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the levy is payable under paragraph 89(1)(a) or (c) on the sale of a

leviable milk product to a person (the _purchaser_); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>there is not in force an agreement under clause&#160;103 that relates to

the payment of levy by the purchaser.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>For better securing the payment of the levy:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person who performed the last process in relation to the product

before the sale occurred is, by force of this clause, the agent of the

Commonwealth for the purposes of the collection of the levy; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the collection agent supplied the product directly to the

purchaser&#151;payment of the levy is to be made to the collection agent on behalf

of the Commonwealth at or before the time when the levy becomes due to be paid.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If the purchaser pays an amount of levy under paragraph&#160;(2)(b), the

purchaser is, to the extent of the amount so paid, discharged from liability to

pay the levy to the Commonwealth.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Remission of levy by agent_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>If the collection agent receives an amount of levy under

paragraph&#160;(2)(b) during a particular month, the agent must remit the levy

to the Commonwealth within:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the agent is a designated small remitter in relation to the financial

year in which the month occurred&#151;28 days after the end of the financial year;

or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>in any other case&#151;28 days after the end of the month.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>A person is guilty of an offence if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person is subject to a requirement to remit levy under

subclause&#160;(4); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the person engages in conduct; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the person's conduct contravenes the requirement.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Penalty:	230 penalty units or imprisonment for 12 months, or both.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Chapter&#160;2 of the _Criminal Code_ sets out the

general principles of criminal responsibility.

 </dl></dl>

_Information about levy_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>If the collection agent supplied the product directly to the purchaser,

the collection agent must, before the levy becomes due to be paid, inform the

purchaser, either on the invoice for the product or in some other way:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>that levy is payable on the sale of the product; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>of the amount of levy payable.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(7)</dt><dd>A person is guilty of an offence if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person is subject to a requirement to inform another person under

subclause&#160;(6); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the first-mentioned person engages in conduct; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the first-mentioned person's conduct contravenes the requirement.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Penalty for contravention of this subclause:	50 penalty units.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Chapter&#160;2 of the _Criminal Code_ sets out the

general principles of criminal responsibility.

 </dl></dl>

98  Collection sub-agents&#151;simple supply chain

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This clause applies to levy if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the levy is payable under paragraph 89(1)(a) or (c) on the sale of a

leviable milk product to a person (the _purchaser_); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the collection agent for the levy supplied the product to the purchaser

indirectly, through a single interposed person; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>there is not in force an agreement under clause&#160;103 that relates to

the payment of levy by the purchaser.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	For example, if the collection agent (A) sells the product

to a wholesaler (W), who in turn sells the product to the purchaser, then W is

the interposed person.

 </dl></dl>

_Payment of levy by the purchaser_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>For better securing the payment of the levy:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the interposed person is, by force of this clause, the sub-agent of the

Commonwealth for the purposes of the collection of the levy; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>payment of the levy is to be made to the collection sub-agent on behalf of

the Commonwealth at or before the time when the levy becomes due to be paid.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If the purchaser pays an amount of levy under paragraph&#160;(2)(b), the

purchaser is, to the extent of the amount so paid, discharged from liability to

pay the levy to the Commonwealth.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

_Remission of levy by sub-agent and agent_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>If the collection sub-agent receives an amount of levy under

paragraph&#160;(2)(b), the sub-agent must remit the levy to the collection

agent by such time as is ascertained in accordance with the regulations.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>If the collection agent receives an amount of levy under subclause&#160;(4) during a particular month, the agent must remit the levy to the Commonwealth within: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the agent is a designated small remitter in relation to the financial

year in which the month occurred&#151;28 days after the end of the financial year;

or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>in any other case&#151;28 days after the end of the month.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>A person is guilty of an offence if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person is subject to a requirement to remit levy under

subclause&#160;(4) or (5); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the person engages in conduct; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the person's conduct contravenes the requirement.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Penalty:	230 penalty units or imprisonment for 12 months, or both.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Chapter&#160;2 of the _Criminal Code_ sets out the

general principles of criminal responsibility.

 </dl></dl>

_Information about levy_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(7)</dt><dd>The collection agent must, before the levy becomes due to be paid, inform

the collection sub-agent, either on the invoice for the product or in some

other way:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>that levy is payable on the sale of the product to the purchaser; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>of the amount of levy payable.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(8)</dt><dd>The collection sub-agent must, before the levy becomes due to be paid,

inform the purchaser, either on the invoice for the product or in some other

way:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>that levy is payable on the sale of the product to the purchaser; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>of the amount of levy payable.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(9)</dt><dd>A person is guilty of an offence if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person is subject to a requirement to inform another person under

subclause&#160;(7) or (8); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the first-mentioned person engages in conduct; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the first-mentioned person's conduct contravenes the requirement.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Penalty for contravention of this subclause:	50 penalty units.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Chapter&#160;2 of the _Criminal Code_ sets out the

general principles of criminal responsibility.

 </dl></dl>

99  Collection sub-agents&#151;complex supply chain

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This clause applies to levy if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the levy is payable under paragraph 89(1)(a) or (c) on the sale of a

leviable milk product to a person (the _purchaser_); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the collection agent for the levy supplied the product to the purchaser

indirectly, through 2 or more interposed persons; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>there is not in force an agreement under clause&#160;103 that relates to

the payment of levy by the purchaser.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

_Supply chain_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>For the purposes of this clause, the interposed persons are taken to form

a _supply chain_, and are to be ranked in an order that corresponds

to the order of those persons in the supply chain, with:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person who acquired the product from the collection agent being ranked

highest; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the person who sold the product to the purchaser being ranked lowest.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	For example, if the collection agent (A) sells the product

to a wholesaler (W) and W sells the product to a distributor (D), who in turn

sells the product to the purchaser, then W is the highest-ranking interposed

person and D is the lowest-ranking interposed person.

 </dl></dl>

_Payment of levy by the purchaser_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>For better securing the payment of the levy:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>each interposed person is, by force of this clause, a sub-agent of the

Commonwealth for the purposes of the collection of the levy; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>payment of the levy is to be made to the lowest-ranking collection

sub-agent on behalf of the Commonwealth at or before the time when the levy

becomes due to be paid.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>If the purchaser pays an amount of levy under paragraph&#160;(3)(b), the

purchaser is, to the extent of the amount so paid, discharged from liability to

pay the levy to the Commonwealth.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Remission of levy by sub-agent and agent_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>If the lowest-ranking collection sub-agent receives an amount of levy

under paragraph&#160;(3)(b), the sub-agent must remit the levy to the next

highest ranking sub-agent in the supply chain by such time as is ascertained in

accordance with the regulations.</dd> <dt>(6)</dt><dd>If a collection sub-agent (other than the highest-ranking sub-agent) receives an amount of levy under subclause&#160;(5) or this subclause, the sub-agent must remit the levy to the next highest ranking sub-agent in the supply chain by such time as is ascertained in accordance with the regulations.</dd> <dt>(7)</dt><dd>If the highest-ranking collection sub-agent receives an amount of levy under subclause&#160;(5) or (6), the sub-agent must remit the levy to the collection agent by such time as is ascertained in accordance with the regulations.</dd> <dt>(8)</dt><dd>If the collection agent receives an amount of levy under subclause&#160;(7) during a particular month, the agent must remit the levy to the Commonwealth within: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the agent is a designated small remitter in relation to the financial

year in which the month occurred&#151;28 days after the end of the financial year;

or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>in any other case&#151;28 days after the end of the month.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(9)</dt><dd>A person is guilty of an offence if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person is subject to a requirement to remit levy under

subclause&#160;(5), (6), (7) or (8); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the person engages in conduct; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the person's conduct contravenes the requirement.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Penalty:	230 penalty units or imprisonment for 12 months, or both.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Chapter&#160;2 of the _Criminal Code_ sets out the

general principles of criminal responsibility.

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

_Information about levy_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(10)</dt><dd>The collection agent must, before the levy becomes due to be paid, inform

the highest-ranking collection sub-agent, either on the invoice for the product

or in some other way:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>that levy is payable on the sale of the product to the purchaser; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>of the amount of levy payable.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(11)</dt><dd>A collection sub-agent (other than the lowest-ranking sub-agent) must,

before the levy becomes due to be paid, inform the next lowest-ranking

collection sub-agent, either on the invoice for the product or in some other

way:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>that levy is payable on the sale of the product to the purchaser; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>of the amount of levy payable.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(12)</dt><dd>The lowest-ranking collection sub-agent must, before the levy becomes due

to be paid, inform the purchaser, either on the invoice for the product or in

some other way:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>that levy is payable on the sale of the product to the purchaser; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>of the amount of levy payable.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(13)</dt><dd>A person is guilty of an offence if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person is subject to a requirement to inform another person under

subclause&#160;(10), (11) or (12); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the first-mentioned person engages in conduct; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the first-mentioned person's conduct contravenes the requirement.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Penalty for contravention of this subclause:	50 penalty units.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Chapter&#160;2 of the _Criminal Code_ sets out the

general principles of criminal responsibility.

 </dl></dl>

100  Collection agents and collection sub-agents to notify unpaid levy

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an amount of levy is required to be paid to a collection agent or a

collection sub-agent under paragraph 97(2)(b), 98(2)(b) or 99(3)(b) at or

before a particular time in a particular month; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the levy is not paid at or before that time;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the collection agent or collection sub-agent must, within 28 days after the end of the month, give an authorised person a notice about the unpaid levy. 

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>A notice under subclause&#160;(1) must set out such information as is

specified in the regulations.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>A person is guilty of an offence if: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person is subject to a requirement to give an authorised person a

notice under subclause&#160;(1); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the first-mentioned person engages in conduct; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the first-mentioned person's conduct contravenes the requirement.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

Penalty for contravention of this subclause:	50 penalty units.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Chapter&#160;2 of the _Criminal Code_ sets out the

general principles of criminal responsibility.

 </dl></dl>

101  Collection agents and collection sub-agents to notify unremitted levy

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an amount of levy is required by subclause 98(4) or 99(5), (6) or (7) to

be remitted to a collection agent or a collection sub-agent by a particular

time in a particular month; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the levy is not remitted by that time;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the collection agent or collection sub-agent must, within 28 days after the end of the month, give an authorised person a notice about the unremitted levy. 

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>A notice under subclause&#160;(1) must set out such information as is

specified in the regulations.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>A person is guilty of an offence if: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person is subject to a requirement to give an authorised person a

notice under subclause&#160;(1); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the first-mentioned person engages in conduct; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the first-mentioned person's conduct contravenes the requirement.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Penalty for contravention of this subclause:	50 penalty units.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Chapter&#160;2 of the _Criminal Code_ sets out the

general principles of criminal responsibility.

 </dl></dl>

102  Collection agents and collection sub-agents to issue receipts for levy

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If a collection agent receives an amount of levy from another person under

paragraph 97(2)(b) or subclause 98(4) or 99(7), the agent must give the other

person a receipt for the levy within 14 days after receiving the levy.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>If a collection sub-agent receives an amount of levy from another person under paragraph 98(2)(b) or 99(3)(b) or subclause 99(5) or (6), the sub-agent must give the other person a receipt for the levy within 14 days after receiving the levy.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>The regulations may make provision for exemptions from subclause&#160;(1) or (2).</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>A receipt given under this clause must contain such information as is specified in the regulations.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>A person is guilty of an offence if: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person is subject to a requirement to give a receipt to another person

under subclause&#160;(1) or (2); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the first-mentioned person engages in conduct; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the first-mentioned person's conduct contravenes the requirement.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Penalty:	50 penalty units.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Chapter&#160;2 of the _Criminal Code_ sets out the

general principles of criminal responsibility.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>For the purposes of this clause, a _receipt_ means an

acknowledgment of having received levy, whether that acknowledgment is given:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>in writing; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>by way of electronic transmission; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>in any other form;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

but does not include a verbal acknowledgment. 

103  Collecting organisations

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This clause applies to levy payable under paragraph 89(1)(a) or (c) on the

sale of a leviable milk product.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The Secretary may enter into an agreement with an organisation with respect to the collection, on behalf of the Commonwealth, of levy by that organisation.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>The matters that may be provided for in an agreement entered into with a collecting organisation include (but are not limited to): </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the State or region in which amounts of levy are to be collected by the

organisation; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the persons from whom amounts of levy are to be collected by the

organisation; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the keeping by the organisation of accounts and records in relation to

amounts of levy collected by the organisation; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the remission by the organisation to the Commonwealth of amounts of levy

collected by the organisation; and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>the giving by the organisation to the Secretary of information about:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

	(i)	amounts of levy collected by the organisation; and
 	(ii)	amounts of levy remitted by the organisation to the Commonwealth; and
 	(iii)	leviable milk products in respect of which levy is payable; and

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>the inspection and audit of accounts and records kept by the organisation

for the purposes of paragraph&#160;(c).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>If an agreement entered into under subclause&#160;(1) with a collecting

organisation is in force in relation to the payment of levy by a particular

person, payment of levy payable by that person is to be made to that

organisation, on behalf of the Commonwealth, in accordance with the terms of

the agreement.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>If a person pays an amount of levy in accordance with subclause&#160;(4), the person is, to the extent of the amount so paid, discharged from liability to pay the levy to the Commonwealth.</dd> <dt>(6)</dt><dd>Before making an agreement under subclause&#160;(1), the Secretary must consult the Council.</dd> <dt>(7)</dt><dd>The Secretary must give notice in the _Gazette_ of the making of an agreement under subclause&#160;(1) within 21 days after the making of the agreement.</dd> <dt>(8)</dt><dd>A failure to comply with subclause&#160;(6) or (7) does not invalidate the agreement.</dd> <dt>(9)</dt><dd>The Commonwealth must not, in exercising its powers under this clause: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>discriminate between States or parts of States within the meaning of

subparagraph 51(ii) of the Constitution; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>give preference to one State or any part thereof within the meaning of

section&#160;99 of the Constitution.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

104  Application of the _Financial Management and Accountability Act 1997_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The _Financial Management and Accountability Act 1997_ does not apply

in relation to levy collected by a collection agent, a collection sub-agent or

a collecting organisation.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The operation of the _Financial Management and Accountability Act 1997_ in relation to money remitted by a collection agent or a collecting organisation to the Commonwealth is not affected by subclause&#160;(1). </dd> </dl></dl>

Division&#160;5&#151;Record-keeping requirements 
 105  Record-keeping requirements for levy payers

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If levy is payable under paragraph 89(1)(a) or (c) on the sale of a

leviable milk product, the purchaser of the product must:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>keep a record of the sale; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>retain that record for at least 5 years after the sale.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If levy is payable under paragraph 89(1)(b) on the retail sale of a

leviable milk product, the retail seller must:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>keep a record of the sale; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>retain that record for at least 5 years after the sale.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If levy is payable under paragraph 89(1)(d) on the relevant application to

a person's own use of a leviable milk product, the person must:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>keep a record of that relevant application; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>retain that record for at least 5 years after the completion of the

relevant application.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>A record kept under this clause must be:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>in English, or readily accessible and easily convertible into English;

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>such as to enable the person's liability for levy to be readily

ascertained.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>However, it is not necessary for a person to retain records under this

clause if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the Secretary notifies the person that the person does not need to retain

the records; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the person is a company that has been finally dissolved.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>A person is guilty of an offence if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person is subject to a requirement to keep or retain a record under

this clause; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the person engages in conduct; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the person's conduct contravenes the requirement.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Penalty for contravention of this subclause:	 30 penalty units.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Chapter&#160;2 of the _Criminal Code_ sets out the

general principles of criminal responsibility.

 </dl></dl>

106  Record-keeping requirements for collection agents and collection sub-agents

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If a collection agent receives an amount of levy under paragraph 97(2)(b)

or subclause 98(4) or 99(7), the agent must:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>keep a record of the receipt; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>retain that record for at least 5 years after the receipt.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If a collection sub-agent receives an amount of levy under paragraph

98(2)(b) or 99(3)(b) or subclause 99(5) or (6), the sub-agent must:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>keep a record of the receipt; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>retain that record for at least 5 years after the receipt.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>A record kept under this clause must be:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>in English, or readily accessible and easily convertible into English;

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>such as to enable the agent's or sub-agent's liability to remit levy to be

readily ascertained.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>However, it is not necessary for a person to retain records under this

clause if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the Secretary notifies the person that the person does not need to retain

the records; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the person is a company that has been finally dissolved.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>A person is guilty of an offence if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person is subject to a requirement to keep or retain a record under

this clause; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the person engages in conduct; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the person's conduct contravenes the requirement.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Penalty for contravention of this subclause:	 30 penalty units.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Chapter&#160;2 of the _Criminal Code_ sets out the

general principles of criminal responsibility.

 </dl></dl>

Division&#160;6&#151;Late payment penalty 
 107  Late payment penalty

_Late payments by levy payer_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If an amount of levy that is payable by a person remains unpaid after the

time when it became due for payment, there is payable by the person to the

Commonwealth, by way of penalty accruing from the time the levy became due for

payment until it is paid in full, an amount worked out as follows:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>during the month in which the levy became due for payment, the amount of

penalty accrues at the rate of 2% per month on the levy due;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>during the next and each subsequent month, the amount of penalty consists

of the sum of:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

	(i)	each amount that accrued during a previous month; and
 	(ii)	the amount accruing during that month at the rate of 2% per month on the sum of the amount of levy then payable and penalty payable at the end of the previous month.

_Late remission by collection agent or collection sub-agent_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If an amount of levy that is required by clause&#160;97, 98 or 99 to be

remitted by a collection agent or a collection sub-agent remains unremitted

after the time when it was required to be remitted, there is payable by the

agent or sub-agent to the Commonwealth, by way of penalty accruing from the

time the levy was required to be remitted until it is remitted in full, an

amount worked out as follows:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>during the month in which the levy was required to be remitted, the amount

of penalty accrues at the rate of 2% per month on the unremitted levy;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>during the next and each subsequent month, the amount of penalty consists

of the sum of:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

	(i)	each amount that accrued during a previous month; and
 	(ii)	the amount accruing during that month at the rate of 2% per month on the sum of the levy then unremitted and penalty payable at the end of the previous month.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The Secretary may extinguish a person's liability for the whole or a part

of an amount of penalty payable under this clause.

</dd> </dl></dl>

Division&#160;7&#151;Recovery of levy debts 
 108  Levy debts

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>For the purposes of this Division, a _levy debt_ is:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an amount of levy that is due and payable by a person; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>an amount of levy that is required by clause&#160;97, 98 or 99 to be

remitted to the Commonwealth by a collection agent and that remains unremitted

after the time when it is required to be remitted; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>an amount of levy that is required by clause&#160;98 or 99 to be remitted

to a collection agent by a collection sub-agent and that remains unremitted

after the time when it is required to be remitted; or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>an amount of levy that is required by clause&#160;99 to be remitted to a

collection sub-agent by another collection sub-agent and that remains

unremitted after the time when it is required to be remitted; or</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>an amount of levy that is required by an agreement under clause&#160;103

to be remitted to the Commonwealth by a collecting organisation and that

remains unremitted after the time when it is required to be remitted; or</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>an amount of late payment penalty.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If an amount of levy that was required to be remitted is recovered by the

Commonwealth under this Division:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the obligation to remit the amount of levy ceases from the time of the

recovery; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>subclause 108(2) has effect as if the amount of levy had been remitted at

the time of the recovery.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

109  Levy debts are debts due to the Commonwealth

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		A levy debt is a debt due to the Commonwealth.

 </dl></dl>

110  Recovery of levy debts

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		A levy debt may be recovered by the Commonwealth by action in a court of

competent jurisdiction.

 </dl></dl>

111  Commonwealth may collect money from a person who owes money to a person

_What this clause does_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This clause allows the Commonwealth to collect money from a person who

owes money to a person that has a levy debt.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_The Secretary may give direction_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The Secretary may direct a person (the _third party_) who

owes, or may later owe, money (the _available money_) to the person

to pay some or all of the available money to the Commonwealth in accordance

with the direction. The Secretary must give a copy of the direction to the

person.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Limit on directions_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The direction cannot require an amount to be paid to the Commonwealth at a

time before it becomes owing by the third party to the person.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

_Third party to comply_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>The third party must comply with the direction.

</dd> </dl></dl>

Penalty:	20 penalty units.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Chapter&#160;2 of the _Criminal Code_ sets out the

general principles of criminal responsibility.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>The third party is not guilty of an offence against subclause&#160;(4) if

the third party complies with the direction so far as the third party is able

to do so.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	A defendant bears an evidential burden in relation to the

matter in subclause&#160;(5). See subsection 13.3(3) of the _Criminal Code_.

 </dl></dl>

_Court orders_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>If a person is convicted of an offence in relation to a refusal or failure

of the third party to comply with subclause&#160;(4), the court may (in

addition to imposing a penalty on the convicted person) order the convicted

person to pay to the Commonwealth an amount up to the amount involved in the

refusal or failure of the third party.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Indemnity_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(7)</dt><dd>Any payment made by the third party under this clause is taken to have

been made with the authority of the person and of all other persons concerned,

and the third party is indemnified for the payment.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Notice_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(8)</dt><dd>If the whole of the levy debt of the person is discharged before any

payment is made by the third party, the Secretary must immediately give notice

to the third party of that fact.</dd> <dt>(9)</dt><dd>If a part of the levy debt of the person is discharged before any payment is made by the third party, the Secretary must: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>immediately give notice to the third party of that fact; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>make an appropriate variation to the direction; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>give a copy of the varied direction to the person.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_When third party is taken to owe money_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(10)</dt><dd>The third party is taken to owe money to the person if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>money is due or accruing by the third party to the person; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the third party holds money for or on account of the person; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the third party holds money on account of some other person for payment to

the person; or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the third party has authority from some other person to pay money to the

person;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

whether or not the payment of the money to the person is dependent on a pre-condition that has not been fulfilled.

Division&#160;8&#151;Information-gathering powers 
 112  Power to call for returns or information

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>An authorised person may, by notice in writing given to a person, require

the person:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>to give the authorised person, within such reasonable time as is specified

in the notice, such return or information in relation to matters relevant to

the operation of this Part as is specified in the notice; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>to verify any such return or information by statutory declaration.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>A person is guilty of an offence if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person has been given a notice under subclause&#160;(1); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the person engages in conduct; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the person's conduct contravenes a requirement in the notice.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Penalty:	60 penalty units.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Chapter&#160;2 of the _Criminal Code_ sets out the

general principles of criminal responsibility.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If a person is convicted of an offence against subclause&#160;(2):

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the court may direct the person to give the return or information that he

or she is required to give; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>on being so directed, the person must give the return or information to an

authorised person within the time specified in the direction.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>A person is guilty of an offence if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person has been given a direction under subclause&#160;(3); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the person engages in conduct; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the person's conduct contravenes a requirement in the direction.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Penalty for contravention of this subclause:	60 penalty units.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Chapter&#160;2 of the _Criminal Code_ sets out the

general principles of criminal responsibility.

 </dl></dl>

113  Regulations may require the giving of returns or information

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The regulations may require any or all of the following persons to give

returns or information for the purposes of this Part:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>persons who are liable to pay, or who have paid, levy;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>collection agents;</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>collection sub-agents;</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>such other persons as are prescribed.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The regulations may prescribe penalties, not exceeding a fine of 50

penalty units, for offences against regulations made for the purposes of

subclause&#160;(1).</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>If a person is convicted of an offence against regulations made for the purposes of this clause: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the court may direct the person to give the return or information that he

or she is required to give; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>on being so directed, the person must give the return or information to an

authorised person within the time specified in the direction.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>A person is guilty of an offence if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person has been given a direction under subclause&#160;(3); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the person engages in conduct; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the person's conduct contravenes a requirement in the direction.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Penalty for contravention of this subclause:	60 penalty units.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Chapter&#160;2 of the _Criminal Code_ sets out the

general principles of criminal responsibility.

 </dl></dl>

114  Self-incrimination

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>An individual is not excused from submitting a return or giving

information under this Division on the ground that the return or information

might tend to incriminate the individual or expose the individual to a

penalty.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>However: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>submitting the return or giving the information; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>any information, document or thing obtained as a direct or indirect

consequence of submitting the return or giving the information;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

is not admissible in evidence against the individual in criminal proceedings other than:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>proceedings for an offence against subclause 112(2) or (4) or 113(4); or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>proceedings for an offence against regulations made for the purposes of

clause&#160;113; or</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>proceedings for an offence against section&#160;137.1 or 137.2 of the

_Criminal Code_ that relates to this Division.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>In this clause:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_this Division_ includes regulations made for the purposes of

clause&#160;113.

 </dl></dl>

Division&#160;9&#151;Access to premises 
 115  Powers of authorised person in relation to premises

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>An authorised person may:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>with the consent of the occupier or person in charge of premises; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>in accordance with a warrant issued under clause&#160;118 in relation to

premises;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

enter the premises for the purpose of ascertaining whether a person has contravened or is contravening a provision of this Part.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If an authorised person enters any premises under subclause&#160;(1), the

authorised person may:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>search the premises for, examine and take stock of, any leviable milk

products; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>search the premises for, inspect, examine, take extracts from, and make

copies of, any examinable documents.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

116  Obstruction of authorised person acting under a warrant

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A person is guilty of an offence if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person obstructs or hinders an authorised person in the exercise of

the authorised person's power under clause&#160;115; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the authorised person exercises that power in accordance with a warrant

issued under clause&#160;118.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Penalty:	30 penalty units.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Chapter&#160;2 of the _Criminal Code_ sets out the

general principles of criminal responsibility.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>In paragraph&#160;(1)(a), strict liability applies to the physical element

of circumstance, that the authorised person's power is under clause&#160;115.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	For strict liability, see section&#160;6.1 of the

_Criminal Code_.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>In paragraph&#160;(1)(b), strict liability applies to the physical element

of circumstance, that the issue of the warrant was under clause&#160;118.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	For strict liability, see section&#160;6.1 of the

_Criminal Code_.

 </dl></dl>

117  Persons to assist authorised persons acting under a warrant

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If an authorised person enters any premises under clause&#160;115 in

accordance with a warrant issued under clause&#160;118, the occupier or the

person in charge must, if requested to do so by the authorised person, provide

reasonable assistance to the authorised person in the exercise of his or her

power under that clause in relation to those premises.</dd> <dt>(1A)</dt><dd>In subclause&#160;(1), strict liability applies to the physical elements of circumstance, that: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the authorised person's power is under clause&#160;115; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the issue of the warrant was under clause&#160;118.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	For strict liability, see section&#160;6.1 of the

_Criminal Code_.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>A person is guilty of an offence if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person is subject to a requirement to provide reasonable assistance to

an authorised person under subclause&#160;(1); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the first-mentioned person engages in conduct; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the first-mentioned person's conduct contravenes the requirement.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Penalty for contravention of this subclause:	30 penalty units.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Chapter&#160;2 of the _Criminal Code_ sets out the

general principles of criminal responsibility.

 </dl></dl>

118  Warrant to enter premises

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If a magistrate, on application by an authorised person, is satisfied, by

information on oath:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>that there are reasonable grounds for believing:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

	(i)	that there are on particular premises any leviable milk products; or
 	(ii)	that there are examinable documents on particular premises; and

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>that the issue of the warrant is reasonably required for the purpose of

ascertaining whether a person has contravened or is contravening a provision of

this Part;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the magistrate may issue a warrant authorising the authorised person to enter the premises:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>with such assistance, and by such force, as is necessary and reasonable;

and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>during such hours as the warrant specifies, or, if the warrant so

specifies, at any time.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>A warrant must specify:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the powers exercisable under subclause 115(2) by the authorised person to

whom the warrant is issued; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the day (not more than 14 days after the issue of the warrant) on which

the warrant ceases to have effect.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

119  Identity cards

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The Secretary may cause an identity card to be issued to an authorised

person.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>An identity card must: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>contain a recent photograph of the authorised person to whom it is issued;

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>be in a form approved, in writing, by the Secretary.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>A person is guilty of an offence if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person has been issued with an identity card under subclause&#160;(1);

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the person ceases to be an authorised person for the purposes of this

Division; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the person does not immediately return the identity card to the Secretary.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Penalty:	1 penalty unit.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Chapter&#160;2 of the _Criminal Code_ sets out the

general principles of criminal responsibility.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>If an authorised person proposes to enter premises otherwise than in

accordance with a warrant issued under clause&#160;118:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the authorised person must produce his or her identity card to the

occupier or the person in charge of the premises for inspection; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the authorised person fails to do so, the authorised person is not

entitled to enter the premises under clause&#160;115.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Division&#160;10&#151;Evidentiary certificates 
 120  Evidentiary certificates

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The Secretary may issue a written certificate:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>stating that a person is liable to pay levy in respect of one or more

sales of leviable milk products; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>setting out particulars of those sales.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The Secretary may issue a written certificate:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>stating that a person is liable to pay levy in respect of one or more

relevant applications to the person's own use of leviable milk products; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>setting out particulars of those relevant applications.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The Secretary may issue a written certificate:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>stating that a specified person has contravened a levy remission

provision; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>setting out particulars of that contravention.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>In this clause:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_levy remission provision_ means:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>subclause 97(4); or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>subclause 98(4); or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>subclause 98(5); or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>subclause 99(5); or</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>subclause 99(6); or</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>subclause 99(7); or</dd>

<dt>(g)</dt><dd>subclause 99(8).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

121  Evidentiary effect of certificate

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>In any civil proceedings under, or arising out of, this Part, a

certificate under clause&#160;120 is prima facie evidence of the matters in the

certificate.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>A document purporting to be a certificate under clause&#160;120 must, unless the contrary is established, be taken to be such a certificate and to have been properly issued.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>The Secretary may certify that a document is a copy of a certificate under clause&#160;120.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>This clause applies to the certified copy as if it were the original. </dd> </dl></dl>

Division&#160;11&#151;Miscellaneous 
 122  Designated small remitters

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The Secretary may, by written notice given to a person, declare that the

person is a _designated small remitter_ in relation to a specified

financial year for the purposes of this Part.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The declaration has effect accordingly.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>The Secretary must not make a declaration in relation to a person under subclause&#160;(1) unless the Secretary is satisfied that: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person has received, or is likely to receive, one or more amounts of

levy in the capacity of collection agent during the financial year concerned;

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the total of those amounts is, or is likely to be, less than $1,000.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

123  Designated small levy-payers

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The Secretary may, by written notice given to a person, declare that the

person is a _designated small levy-payer_ in relation to a

specified financial year for the purposes of this Part.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The declaration has effect accordingly.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>The Secretary must not make a declaration in relation to a person under subclause&#160;(1) unless the Secretary is satisfied that: </dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person is liable to pay, or is likely to be liable to pay either or

both of the following:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

	(i)	one or more amounts of levy under paragraph 89(1)(b) on retail sales that occurred, or are likely to occur, during that financial year;
 	(ii)	one or more amounts of levy under paragraph 89(1)(d) on relevant applications that occurred, or are likely to occur, during the financial year concerned; and 

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the total of those amounts is, or is likely to be, less than $1,000.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

124  Refund of overpayments

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If any of the following amounts has been overpaid, the amount overpaid must

be refunded by the Commonwealth:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an amount of levy;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>an amount of late payment penalty.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

125  Refund of levy

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The regulations may make provision for refunds of levy.

 </dl></dl>

126  Methods by which levy may be paid or remitted

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The regulations may make provision for the methods by which levy may be

paid or remitted to the Commonwealth.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>Regulations made for the purposes of this clause may make provision for levy to be paid or remitted using an electronic funds transfer system. </dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>Subclause&#160;(2) does not limit subclause&#160;(1). </dd> </dl></dl>

127  Authorised persons

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The Secretary may, by writing, authorise a specified APS employee to be an

authorised person for the purposes of a specified provision or provisions of

this Part.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The Secretary must not authorise an APS employee under subclause&#160;(1) unless the Secretary is of the opinion that the holder for the time being of the position held by the employee is reasonably likely to be suitably qualified (because of ability and experience) to be an authorised person for the purposes of the provision or provisions concerned.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>The Secretary may, by writing, authorise a specified person employed by, or in the service of, a collecting organisation to be an authorised person for the purposes of clause&#160;112\. </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Clause&#160;112 deals with the giving of returns or

information.

 </dl></dl>

128  Publication of information about levy

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>An authorised person may publish:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the name and address of a person who has paid, or is liable to pay:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

	(i)	levy; or
 	(ii)	an amount of late payment penalty; or

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the name and address of a collection agent, a collection sub-agent or a

collecting organisation; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>information about amounts of levy received or receivable by the

Commonwealth in any period (including such information relating to a particular

State or region); or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>information about leviable milk products in respect of which levy is

payable;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

to either of the following:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>the Council;</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>a person to whom the Secretary has granted access to such information.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>Subclause&#160;(1) does not authorise the publication of information in a

manner that enables:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an amount of levy paid or payable to be identified with a person

(including a deceased person); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>an amount of late payment penalty paid or payable to be identified with a

person (including a deceased person).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The Secretary may, on behalf of the Commonwealth, charge a fee for

publishing a name, address or information under subclause&#160;(1).</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>The amount of a fee under subclause&#160;(3) must not be such as to amount to taxation. </dd> </dl></dl>

129  Delegation by Secretary

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The Secretary may, by writing, delegate to a senior officer all or any of

the Secretary's powers under this Part (other than clause&#160;127).

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Clause&#160;127 deals with authorised persons.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>A delegate under this clause is, in the exercise of a function or power

delegated under this clause, subject to any directions given by the

Secretary.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>In this clause: </dd> </dl></dl>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_senior officer_ means:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a person who holds or performs the duties of a Senior Executive Service

office or position in the Department; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a person who holds or performs the duties of a DPIE Band 3 office or

position, or an equivalent office or position, in the Department.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

130  Reconsideration and review of decisions

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A person affected by a relevant decision who is dissatisfied with the

decision may, within:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>28 days after the day on which the decision first comes to the notice of

the person; or </dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>such further period as the Secretary (either before or after the end of

the period), by written notice given to the person, allows;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

by written notice given to the Secretary, request the Secretary to reconsider the decision.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>A request under subclause&#160;(1) must set out the reasons for making the

request.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>The Secretary must, within 45 days after receiving a request under subclause&#160;(2), reconsider the relevant decision and may make a decision: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>in substitution for the relevant decision, whether in the same terms as

the relevant decision or not; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>revoking the relevant decision.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>If, as a result of a reconsideration under subclause&#160;(3), the

Secretary makes a decision in substitution for or revoking a relevant decision,

the Secretary must, by written notice given to the person who made the request

under subclause&#160;(1) for the reconsideration, inform the person of the

result of the reconsideration and give the reasons for his or her decision.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>An application may be made to the Administrative Appeals Tribunal for review of a decision of the Secretary under subclause&#160;(3).</dd> <dt>(6)</dt><dd>A person who makes a relevant decision must give to a person affected by the decision a written statement to the effect that a person affected by the decision: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>may, if the person is dissatisfied with the decision, seek a

reconsideration of the decision in accordance with this clause; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>may, subject to the _Administrative Appeals Tribunal Act 1975_, if

the person is dissatisfied with a decision made on that reconsideration, make

application to the Administrative Appeals Tribunal for review of that decision.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(7)</dt><dd>If the Secretary makes a decision under subclause&#160;(3) and gives to a

person affected by the decision notice in writing of the making of the

decision, that notice must include a statement to the effect that, subject to

the _Administrative Appeals Tribunal Act 1975_, application may be made to

the Administrative Appeals Tribunal for review of the decision to which the

notice relates by or on behalf of a person affected by the decision.</dd> <dt>(8)</dt><dd>A failure to comply with subclause&#160;(6) or (7) in relation to a decision does not affect the validity of the decision.</dd> <dt>(9)</dt><dd>In this clause: </dd> </dl></dl>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_relevant decision_ means a decision to refuse to extinguish, under

subclause 107(3), a person's liability for the whole or part of an amount of

late payment penalty.

 </dl></dl>

131  Commonwealth not liable to levy

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The Commonwealth is not liable to pay levy.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>Even though the Commonwealth is not liable to pay levy, it is the intention of the Parliament that the Commonwealth and Commonwealth entities should be notionally liable for levy.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>The Minister for Finance may give such written directions as are necessary or convenient to be given for carrying out or giving effect to subclause&#160;(2) and, in particular, may give directions in relation to the transfer of money within an account, or between accounts, operated by the Commonwealth or a Commonwealth entity.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>Directions under subclause&#160;(3) have effect, and must be complied with, despite any other law of the Commonwealth. </dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>In this clause: </dd> </dl></dl>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_Commonwealth entity_ means:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an Agency (within the meaning of the _Financial Management and Accountability Act 1997_); or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a Commonwealth authority (within the meaning of the _Commonwealth Authorities and Companies Act 1997_);

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

that cannot be made liable to taxation by a Commonwealth law.

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_Minister for Finance_ means the Minister administering the

_Financial Management and Accountability Act 1997_.

 </dl></dl>

Part&#160;5&#151;Offences

133  False or misleading evidence

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		A person is guilty of an offence if:

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person gives evidence to another person; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the person does so knowing that the evidence is false or misleading in a

material particular; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the evidence is given under clause&#160;38.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Penalty:	Imprisonment for 12 months.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Chapter&#160;2 of the _Criminal Code_ sets out the

general principles of criminal responsibility.

 </dl></dl>

<center>**

###  DAIRY PRODUCE ACT 1986<centreit>Notes to the _Dairy Produce Act 1986_ </centreit>
**</center>

**Note 1**

The _Dairy Produce Act 1986_ as shown in this compilation comprises Act No.&#160;54, 1986 amended as indicated in the Tables below. 
 The _Dairy Produce Act 1986_ was modified by the A.C.T. Self-Government (Consequential Provisions) Regulations (Statutory Rules 1989 No.&#160;3 as amended).
 For application, saving or transitional provisions made by the _Corporations (Repeals, Consequentials and Transitionals) Act 2001_, _see_ Act No.&#160;55, 2001.
 All relevant information pertaining to application, saving or transitional provisions prior to 3&#160;April 2000 is not included in this compilation. For subsequent information _see_ Table A.

  </th>
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>32, 2004</div>

  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>Sch. 1 (item 3) \[ <i>see</i>Table A]</div>

  </th>
</tr></table>_(a)_ 
<center>Back to Top</center>
 The _Dairy Produce Act 1986_ was amended by section&#160;3 only of the _Statute Law (Miscellaneous Provisions) Act (No. 2) 1986_, subsection 2(4) of which provides as follows:

	(4)	The amendment of paragraph 36(3)(d) of the _Dairy Produce Act 1986_ made by this Act shall be deemed to have come into operation on 1&#160;July 1986.

_(b)_	The _Dairy Produce Act 1986_ was amended by section&#160;3 only of the _Statute Law (Miscellaneous Provisions) Act 1987_, subsection 2(1) of which provides as follows:

	(1)	Subject to this section, this Act shall come into operation on the day on which it receives the Royal Assent.

_(c)_	The _Dairy Produce Act 1986_ was amended by section&#160;3 only of the _Primary Industries (Recovery of Levy Collection Expenses) Act 1988_, subsection 2(1) of which provides as follows:

	(1)	Subject to sections (2), (3) and (4), this Act commences on the day on which it receives the Royal Assent.

_(d)_	The _Dairy Produce Act 1986_ was amended by section&#160;3 only of the _Primary Industries and Energy Legislation Amendment Act 1988_, subsection 2(1) of which provides as follows:

	(1)	Subject to this section, this Act commences on the day on which it receives the Royal Assent.

_(e)_	The _Dairy Produce Act 1986_ was amended by section&#160;53 only of the _Rural Industries Research Amendment Act 1988_, subsection 2(1) of which provides as follows:

	(1)	Subject to this section, this Act commences on the day on which it receives the Royal Assent.

_(f)_	The _Dairy Produce Act 1986_ was amended by section&#160;3 only of the _Primary Industries and Energy Legislation Amendment Act (No. 2) 1989_, subsection 2(1) of which provides as follows:

	(1)	Subject to this section, this Act commences on the day on which it receives the Royal Assent.

_(g)_	Section&#160;2 of the _Dairy Produce Amendment Act 1996_ provides as follows:

	2	This Act is taken to have commenced on 1&#160;July 1995, immediately after the commencement of the _Dairy Produce Amendment Act 1995_.

_(h)_	The _Dairy Produce Act 1986_ was amended by Schedule&#160;4 (item&#160;57) only of the _Statute Law Revision Act 1996_, subsection 2(1) of which provides as follows:

	(1)	Subject to subsections&#160;(2) and (3), this Act commences on the day on which it receives the Royal Assent.

_(i)_ The _Dairy Produce Act 1986_ was amended by Schedule&#160;2 (items&#160;662-695) only of the _Audit (Transitional and Miscellaneous) Amendment Act 1997_ subsection 2(2) of which provides as follows:

	(2)	Schedules&#160;1, 2 and 4 commence on the same day as the _Financial Management and Accountability Act 1997_.

_(j)_ The _Dairy Produce Act 1986_ was amended by Schedule&#160;11 only of the _Primary Industries Levies and Charges (Consequential Amendments) Act 1999_, subsection 2(1) of which provides as follows:

	(1)	Subject to this section, this Act commences on the commencement of section&#160;1 of the _Primary Industries (Excise) Levies Act 1999_.

_(k)_	The _Dairy Produce Act 1986_ was amended by Schedule&#160;1 (items&#160;359 and 360) only of the _Public Employment (Consequential and Transitional) Amendment Act 1999_, subsections 2(1) and (2) of which provide as follows:

	(1)	In this Act, **_commencing time_** means the time when the _Public Service Act 1999_ commences.
 	(2)	Subject to this section, this Act commences at the commencing time.

_(l)_	The _Dairy Produce Act 1986_ was amended by Schedule&#160;10 (items&#160;71-75) only of the _Corporate Law Economic Reform Program Act 1999_, subsection 2(2)(c) of which provides as follows:

	(2)	The following provisions commence on a day or days to be fixed by Proclamation:

	(c)	the items in Schedules&#160;10, 11 and 12\. 

_(m)_ The _Dairy Produce Act 1986_ was amended by Schedule&#160;3 (item&#160;166) only of the _Corporations (Repeals, Consequentials and Transitionals) Act 2001_, subsection 2(3) of which provides as follows:

	(3)	Subject to subsections&#160;(4) to (10), Schedule&#160;3 commences, or is taken to have commenced, at the same time as the _Corporations Act 2001_.

_(n)_ Subsection 2(1) (item&#160;10) of the _Agriculture, Fisheries and Forestry Legislation Amendment Act (No. 1) 2003_ provides as follows:

	(1)	Each provision of this Act specified in column 1 of the table commences, or is taken to have commenced, on the day or at the time specified in column 2 of the table.
